 Chidambaram has challenged the Delhi High Court's November 15 decision dismissing his bail plea in the apex court
 congress ke is 74 varshiya netaa kii jamaanat apil par sunwaayee ke dauraan pravartan nideshaalay kii ore se solicetre general tushaar mehta ne daawa kiya tha ki purv vitt mantri hiraasat main hone ke baavjood mahatvapurn gavaahon par apana ‘prabhaav' rakhte hai jabaki purv vitt mantri kaa kahana tha ki jaanch agency is tarah ke niraadhaar aarope lagaakar unki pratishtha or kariyar ‘barbaad' nahin kar sakati he
 Opposing Chidambaram's bail plea, Mehta had said that a crime like money laundering is of a serious nature and it does not only affect the economy of the country but also stifles public confidence in the system
 mehta kaa kahana tha ki jaanch ke dauraan nideshaalay ne 12 bank khaaton kii pahchaan kii he jinamein is aparaadh se mili rakam jamaa kii gayi or agency ke paas aisi 12 sampattiyon kaa bhi byoraa he jinhen kai duusare deshon main kharida gaya he
 The Enforcement Directorate had claimed that Chidambaram used the 'influential office' of the Finance Minister for 'personal gain' and seized the proceeds of the crime

 Senior advocate Kapil Sibal, on behalf of Chidambaram, argued that he has been kept in jail for the last 99 days in an 'improper manner' because he is the father of Karthi Chidambaram, the main accused in the INX Media money laundering case There is not a single evidence against him to add
 chidambaram ko pehali baar ienex media bhrashtachar maamle main sibiai ne 21 agast ko giraftaar kiya tha

 The former finance minister is currently in judicial custody till December 11

 railway tikat booking site iarsitisi ne apane yugers kii sahuliyat ke liye ek nai suvidha 'i-wolet' kii shuruyaat kii he
 It acts like a virtual wallet, which the user will be able to use to pay the ticket fee
 yani ab yujar ko tikat ke paise chukaane ke liye debit, credit card yaa phir internet banking kii aavashyaktaa nahin hogi
 What is e-wallet-wallet is a kind of online prepaid account available on irctc's site, in which you can deposit money for booking tickets
 jarurat padane par un rupayon kaa istemaal tikat shulk adaa karne ke liye kiya ja sakegaa
 Now your ticket will be booked soon with the facility of this prepaid account, now your ticket will be booked sooner than before
 yah aapke aam bank acount kii tarah hi he, jahaan aap pehle se jamaa rupee kaa istemaal kharidari ke liye karte hai
 The only difference is that you will be able to use the money deposited in 'e-wallet' only on the IRCTC site
 kaise karen i-wolet ke liye registengar aap tikat book karaane liye i-wolet kaa istemaal karnaa chaahate hai to iske liye aapako i-wolet ke liye registration karana hoga
 Here you have to type your PAN card number and the first word of your name
 iske baad aapke saamne ek online form khulegaa, jahaan aap i-wolet ke liye rupee transfar kar apana password bana sakate hai
 You can also use e-wallet to purchase any other product on the IRCTC site
 i-wolet main aap 100 rupee se lekar 5000 rupee tak jamaa kar sakate hai
 How to use: To avail the facility of e-wallet for online shopping and ticketing, after selecting the product or ticket after login on the site, you have to click on the e-wallet in the payment option
 jahaan apana transicashan password daalane ke baad aap jamaa paison kaa istemaal kar paaenge
 To benefit from e-wallet, till now the payment option we used to book tickets on IRCTC, the site had to be connected to the concerned bank online for payment and go to the gateway payment bank
 isamen kaaphi samay lagata he or kai baar pement fail bhi ho jaataa he
 But now with this new facility IRCTC will have to take payment from its own site, which will save time
 tikat radd karne kii sthiti main bhi ab rifund kiya hua paisa jald hi aapke i-wolet acount main aa jayega
 However, you will not be able to use e-wallet to book tickets on IRCTC from 8:00 am to 12:00 pm

 kya he ipisi kii dhara 376kisi bhi mahila ke saath balaatkaar karne ke aaropee paripisi kii dhara376 ke tahat mukadmaa chalaaya jaataa he
 There is a provision to give a minimum sentence of 7 years and maximum 10 years of rigorous punishment to the guilty if proven guilty
 kai durlabh maamalon main doshi ko umrakaid kii sajaa bhi ja sakati he

 Or he can also be fined

 What is Section 375 of the IPC When a man makes a physical relationship with a woman against her will, it is called rape
 kisi bhi kaaran se sambhog kriya puri hui ho yaa nahin lekin kanuunan vah balaatkaar hi kahalaayegaa
 It is divided into sections 375, 376, 376A, 376B, 376C, 376D according to the different circumstances and category of this crime
 kya dhara 375 kaa matlabaidi koi purush kisi mahila kii ichha ke viruddh, uski sahmati ke bina, use daraa dhamkaakar, uskaa nakli pati banakar, dimagi rup se kamjor yaa pagal mahila ko dhokhaa dekar or uske sharaab yaa anya nashile padaarth ke kaaran hosh main nahin hone par uske saath sambhog karata he to vah balaatkaar hi mana jayega
 If the woman is less than 16 years of age, then the sexual intercourse with or without her consent is also rape
 yahi nahin yadi koi purush apni 15 varsh se kam umr kii patni ke saath sambhog karata he to vah bhi balaatkaar hi he
 In all these situations, the accused can be punished
 har sthiti main lagu hota he yah kanoonupadhara (2) ke antargat bataaya gaya he ki koi police adhikari yaa lok sevak apane pad or shaskeey shakti or sthiti kaa phayda uthaakar uski abhiraksha yaa uski adhinsth mahila adhikari yaa karmchaaree ke saath sambhog karegaa, to vah bhi balaatkaar mana jayega
 This law also applies to prisons, hospitals, state offices, child and women reform homes
 sabhi doshiyon ko kathor karawas kii adhiktam sajaa ho sakati he

 acchhee sehat ke liye ek acchhee or sukun-bhari neend behad ahm hoti he
 Getting less sleep can hurt your health in many ways
 neend kii kami ke kaaran diabetes, stroke or motaape kaa shikaar hone kii sambhaavna sabase zyada hoti he
 Nutritionist Rahila Hasan says that, by getting plenty of sleep, the mind gets peace, digestion remains healthy
 saath hi immune system kii kshamta bhi tej hoti he
 These are the ways to improve sleep 1
 din main ek acchhee nap (jhapai) lemogar aap raat main thik se so nahin pate hai to din main kam se kam se 10 se 20 minute kii neend len
 This will freshen up your mood and you will be able to concentrate properly at work
 ye he surya namaskara kaa sahi tarika, hote hai itane laabh2
 Bathing with lukewarm water Take a bath with lukewarm water for about 20 to 30 minutes before sleeping
 aisa karne se sharir kii mansapeshiyon or tantrikaon ko aaraam miltaa he
 Which makes you sleep well
 darasal, sharir ke texrechar main giravat aane se neend aasaani se aa jaati he
 Therefore, bathing with lukewarm water is very helpful for a good sleep
 3
 Sleep alone Most people do not sleep properly due to changes in lights, sounds and temperature
 iske liye jaruri he ki aap akele sone kii koshish karen
 Because the body-temperature of different people is opposite from each other
 jis kaaran unhen ek acchhee neend ke liye alag-alag temparechar kii jarurat padati he
 Apart from this, if the person sleeping with you has a habit of snoring, then you may have difficulty sleeping
 isliye agar acchhee neend lenaa chaahate hai to akele sone kii koshish karen
 Mother's milk is not necessary for children, this problem is not 4
 sone se pehle eksrasij na karenhaalanki, eksrasij karne se neend acchhee aati he kyonki isse dimag ko shanti milti he
 But avoid sleeping immediately after exercising
 neutrishanist rahila hasan ne bataaya, acchhee neend chaahate hai to apane sone ke samay se kam se kam 3 se 6 ghante pehle hi eksrasij kar len
 Never try to sleep immediately after exercising
 5
 Make changes to the food: Hide the food about 3-4 hours before sleeping
 kyonki khate hi so jane se pet main maujuud acid hamaare sharir kii food pive main pahunch jaataa he
 Due to which you may feel a burning sensation in the chest and you are unable to sleep properly even if you want to
